So the filter manager itself is responsible for ensuring route finalization happens on local replies.\n\nLet me trace the actual execution flow: when the router sends a local reply, it passes a `modify_headers_` callback to the filter manager, which then wraps that callback in a lambda that first calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` and then invokes the original callback. This occurs because the router's `sendLocalReply()` callback explicitly calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()`, and the FilterManager's local reply path unconditionally wraps the callback to call `finalizeResponseHeaders()` again before invoking the user-supplied modifier function.\n\n## Root Cause\n\n**File:** `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc` lines 1072-1078, 1123-1129, 1156-1162\n**Mechanism:** The FilterManager's three local reply methods (`prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain`, `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain`, `sendDirectLocalReply`) create a wrapper lambda that unconditionally calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` before executing the caller-supplied `modify_headers` callback.\n\nWhen the router's `sendLocalReply()` is invoked with a callback that also calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` (e.g., for direct responses), this results in the function being called twice in the same response header processing pipeline.\n\n## Evidence\n\n### Router Filter Local Reply Paths\n\n**File:** `source/common/router/router.cc`\n\n1. **Direct Response (lines 486-503):**\n```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(\n    direct_response->responseCode(),\n    direct_response->responseBody(),\n    [this, direct_response, &request_headers = headers](Http::ResponseHeaderMap& response_headers) -> void {\n      // ... location header logic ...\n      direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders(response_headers, callbacks_->streamInfo());\n    },\n    absl::nullopt,\n    StreamInfo::ResponseCodeDetails::get().DirectResponse);\n```\nThe lambda passed to `sendLocalReply()` explicitly calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` at line 501.\n\n2. **No Cluster Found (line 520):**\n```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(route_entry_->clusterNotFoundResponseCode(), callbacks_->streamInfo());\nmodify_headers_(*headers);\n```\nCalled OUTSIDE the `sendLocalReply()` path, so no double-wrapping occurs.\n\n### FilterManager Local Reply Wrapping\n\n**File:** headers) -> void {\n          if (streamInfo().route() && streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()) {\n            streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()->finalizeResponseHeaders(headers, streamInfo());\n          }\n          if (modify_headers) {\n            modify_headers(headers);\n          }\n        },\n        // ... other functions ...\n    },\n    Utility::LocalReplyData{ /* ... */ });\n```\n\nThis pattern is repeated three times:\n- `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` lines 1072-1078\n- `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` lines 1123-1129\n- `sendDirectLocalReply()` lines 1156-1162\n\nThe FilterManager ALWAYS wraps the `modify_headers` callback to call `finalizeResponseHeaders()` first (lines 1074, 1125, 1158).\n\n### Utility::prepareLocalReply Execution\n\n**File:** FilterManager is invoked, which executes both `finalizeResponseHeaders()` AND the user's `modify_headers` callback.\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **`source/common/router/router.cc`** — Router filter's local reply generation\n2. **`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`** — FilterManager's response header processing\n3. **`source/common/http/utility.cc`** — Header finalization and local reply encoding\n4. **`source/common/router/config_impl.cc`** — Route entry configuration and header parsing\n5. **`source/common/router/header_parser.cc`** — Header parser implementation with `append_action` handling\n6. **`api/envoy/config/core/v3/base.proto`** — `HeaderValueOption` protobuf definition with deprecated `append` field\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n1. **Symptom:** Response header `x-custom-trace` appears twice in access logs for local replies (e.g., 504 Upstream Timeout)\n\n2. **Upstream Cause #1 (Direct Response Path):**\n   - Router detects direct response entry at route/vhost level\n   - Calls `callbacks_->sendLocalReply()` with lambda containing `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call\n   - First invocation of `finalizeResponseHeaders()` occurs INSIDE the router's callback\n\n3. **Intermediate Layer (FilterManager Wrapping):**\n   - Router's callback reaches `FilterManager::sendLocalReply()`\n   - FilterManager does NOT know that the router's callback already calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n   - FilterManager unconditionally wraps ALL `modify_headers` callbacks to call `finalizeResponseHeaders()` first\n\n4. **Upstream Cause #2 (Double Invocation):**\n   - Wrapped lambda is passed to `Utility::prepareLocalReply()`\n   - The wrapped lambda executes:\n     - Call #1 to `finalizeResponseHeaders()` (from FilterManager's wrapper)\n     - Call #2 to `finalizeResponseHeaders()` (from router's original callback)\n\n5. **Header Mutation Details:**\n   - `finalizeResponseHeaders()` calls `header_parser->evaluateHeaders()` for each header parser\n   - `evaluateHeaders()` iterates through configured headers and applies `HeaderValueOption::append_action` logic\n   - With `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` (or default `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`), headers are added via `headers.addReferenceKey()`\n   - Two consecutive calls result in headers being added to the map twice\n\n6. **Root Cause:** The architectural change that moved header finalization responsibility to FilterManager's local reply path created an unintended double-invocation when the router filter also finalizes headers in its callbacks.\n\n## Filter Manager Encode Path\n\n**File:** `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc` lines 1244-1330\n\nThe `FilterManager::encodeHeaders()` method iterates through encoder filters in REVERSE order (line 1253-1305), allowing each filter to modify response headers. However, local replies bypass this iteration:\n\n1. When a local reply is triggered during request decoding, FilterManager prepares the response through `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`\n2. During preparation, the wrapped lambda is called, which applies `finalizeResponseHeaders()` once\n3. Result: Headers are finalized twice before being sent to the encoder filters\n\n## Header Configuration Details\n\n**File:** `source/common/router/header_parser.cc` lines 53-76\n\nThe `HeadersToAddEntry` constructor handles the deprecated `append` BoolValue field:\n\n```cpp\nif (header_value_option.has_append()) {\n  // If 'append' is set, convert to append_action enum\n  append_action_ = header_value_option.append().value()\n                       ? When `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is called twice, both invocations use `addReferenceKey()` (line 211 in header_parser.cc), resulting in duplicate header values in the response.\n\n## Complete Causal Chain\n\n```\nUser Configures Route with response_headers_to_add\n         ↓\n[Request processed by Router filter]\n         ↓\n[Router detects condition: timeout/connection failure/no cluster/direct response]\n         ↓\nRouter calls callbacks_->sendLocalReply(..., modify_headers_callback, ...)\n         ↓\n[For DIRECT RESPONSE case] modify_headers_callback includes finalizeResponseHeaders() call\n         ↓\n[FilterManager::sendLocalReply receives the callback]\n         ↓\nFilterManager wraps callback:\n  wrapped_lambda() {\n    finalizeResponseHeaders()  // Call #1 (FilterManager adds this)\n    modify_headers(headers)    // Calls router's callback\n  }\n         ↓\nUtility::prepareLocalReply calls wrapped_lambda()\n         ↓\n[Inside wrapped_lambda]\nCall #1: FilterManager's finalizeResponseHeaders() executes\n         → header_parser->evaluateHeaders() processes response_headers_to_add\n         → For each header: headers.addReferenceKey() adds header to map\n         ↓\nCall #2: Router's modify_headers() callback executes\n         → Which also contains direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()\n         → header_parser->evaluateHeaders() processes response_headers_to_add AGAIN\n         → For each header: headers.addReferenceKey() adds header to map AGAIN\n         ↓\nResult: Each configured header appears TWICE in the response\n         ↓\nAccess log displays: \"x-custom-trace: abc123\" appears twice in response headers\n```\n\n## Recommendation\n\n**Fix Strategy:**\n\nThe FilterManager should NOT unconditionally call `finalizeResponseHeaders()` in its local reply path when the caller's `modify_headers` callback will do so. Options include:\n\n1. **Option A (Cleanest):** Remove the `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call from FilterManager's local reply wrapper lambda. Let the caller (router) be responsible for calling `finalizeResponseHeaders()` through its own callback. Update the \"no cluster found\" path in router to also include `finalizeResponseHeaders()` in its callback.\n\n2. **Option B:** Create a separate callback mechanism for \"already finalized\" headers vs \"needs finalization\" headers, allowing FilterManager to distinguish when finalization has already been performed.\n\n3. **Option C:** Modify the router's direct response path to NOT include `finalizeResponseHeaders()` in its callback, and let FilterManager handle all finalization. This requires ensuring the \"no cluster found\" and other local reply paths also pass callbacks WITHOUT embedded finalization calls.\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Add conditional logging to `finalizeResponseHeaders()` to track call stack and identify double invocations:\n   ```\n   ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(warn, \"finalizeResponseHeaders() called, stack: {}\", *this, stack_trace());\n   ```\n\n2. Count header additions using `headers.addReferenceKey()` to verify duplicate insertions\n\n3.
